     <h2 class="white">
      Experience The Passion &amp;  Care That Defines Us
     </h2>
     <h3 class="white">
      We are a unique medical practice proudly offering premium and personalized care, under the care of Dr. Jodie Reinertson.
     </h3>
     <a href="#doc">
      <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down">
      </i>
     </a>
    </div>
   </div>
   <section class="doc will-parallax parallax1 b-lazy" data-src="https://www.seattlecosmedicskincare.com/wp-content/themes/rm-seattlecosmedicskincare/images/bg-doc.jpg" id="doc">
    <h2 class="black">
     With Us, Itâ€™s Personal
    </h2>
    <h3>
     Sustainable beauty is not about looking artificially young, or frozen, but about allowing your appearance to represent the youthfulness you feel inside.
    </h3>
    <div class="doc-wrapper">
     <div class="doctor-content">
      <p>
       CosMedic Skincare is a boutique, non-surgical practice offering compassionate care from our
       <a href="https://www.seattlecosmedicskincare.com/about/cosmetic-dermatology/">
        doctor
       </a>
       , Jodie Reinertson, MD, and top-notch medical aestheticians. Our expertise is determined by years of experience, education, and a desire to provide the best patient care and customer service to our Seattle-based patients. We specialize in aesthetic medicine and medical weight loss, and customize each treatment to ensure expert care.
      </p>
      <p>
       As a unique medical practice, located in the First Hill neighborhood of Downtown Seattle, we proudly offer premium and personalized skin care solutions. Our therapies and private label medical-grade products are as beneficial to your skinâ€™s overall health as they are to your outward beauty. Along with our breakthrough anti-aging therapies, such as
       <a href="https://www.seattlecosmedicskincare.com/treatments/injectables/botox-wrinkles/">
        BOTOX
       </a>
       Â® Cosmetic and laser skin rejuvenation, we are pleased to offer state-of-the-art
       <a href="https://www.seattlecosmedicskincare.com/treatments/acne/">
        acne treatments
       </a>
       , post-acne scar revision, and pigmentation correction, as well as physician-supervised weight loss.
      </p>
      <p>
       We treat men, women, and teens in an environment that promotes comfort and the best in patient care. Come experience the passion and care that defines us at CosMedic Skincare.
      </p>
      <a class="button" href="https://www.seattlecosmedicskincare.com/about/our-clinic/" rel="nofollow">
       More About Us
      </a>
